 chalane kii gati main karen badlaav-kai study main sabit ho chukaa he ki walk karne se calories bern hoti hai

 2

 vimaanan or prasaaran kshetra main bhi videshi nivesh ko udaar banaaya gaya
 The price of diesel was partially decontrolled and limited supply of subsidized LPG cylinders
 pashchim bengal kii mukhyamantri mamata banerjee ke rajyon ko kendriya sahaayta ke aavanton main bhedbhaav barte jane ke aaropon ke bare main puche gaye ek sawaal par vittamantri ne kaha ki is tarah ke aarope sahi nahin hai
 Whatever money is given to the states is given according to the arrangement made in the Constitution and the recommendations of the Financial Commission
 chidambaram ne kaha, kisi bhi rajya ko na to praathamikta di jaati he or na hi kisi ke saath bhedbhaav kiya jaataa he
 The allegations of discrimination are wrong and i reject these allegations
 bihar, urisa tathaa kuch anya rajyon ko vishesh rajya kaa darja die jane sambandhi sawaal par chidambaram ne kaha, unhone kabhi bhi rajyon ko vishesh darja die jane ke vichaar kaa samarthan nahin kiya he
 However, the government has asked the 14th Finance Commission constituted under the chairmanship of former Reserve Bank of India Governor YV Reddy to give necessary suggestions to the government keeping in mind the problem of debt-burdened states
 vittamantri ne rajyon se kaha he ki unhen majboot banane ke liye behatar parivesh banane ke saath hi kanoon evam vyavastha kii sthiti main sudhaar laana hoga or aarthik gatividhiyon ko protsaahan dena chahie
 Chidambaram said that under the auction process of market regulator Sebi, the current process of setting limits for companies to raise funds through bonds can be replaced by the process adopted in infrastructure (infra) bonds
 tippaniyan He said that the government bond limit would be increased whenever needed
 unhone kaha, companiyon ke bond main videshi sansthagat niveshkon ke liye tay nivesh seemaa kaa 80 pratishat tak jab nivesh pahunch jayega tab sarkaar bade niveshkon kii niveshyojna kii suvidha ke liye videshi nivesh seemaa kii samiksha karegi
 Giving investors a direction, the Finance Minister said, "I am happy that the annual limit for expansion of investment in government bonds remains within the five per cent range of the government's gross borrowings from the market
" haalanki, isamen vaapasi kharid ko alag rakhaa gaya he
 In the case of the global economy, Chidambaram said that the Eurozone crisis has affected investment activities across the world and India has not remained untouched
 unhone yaad dilaate hue kaha ki varsh 2010-11 main aarthik vruddhi ke 9
 After reaching 3 percent, the economy slowed down and in 2011-12 it decreased to 6
 2 pratishat rah gai or ab chaalu vitt varsh ke dauraan iske pichley ek dashak kii nunatam vruddhi 5 pratishat ke daayre main rahane kaa anumaan lagaaya gaya he
 Inaugurating the National Editors' Conference, Chidambaram said that economic reform is a process going forward
 sarkaar ne haal hi main anek kshetron main pratyaksh videshi nivesh ko udaar banane ke saath hi or kai upaay kiye hai
 The government has gone a long way towards furthering reforms and fiscal consolidation
 vitt mantri ne kaha ki videshi sansthagat niveshkon (exai) ke liye nivesh niyamon ko or saral banaaya gaya he
 For them, investment rules in government securities and corporate sector debt instruments have been liberalized
 unhone kaha, 1 april 2013 se exai nivesh ke liye maujuuda alag-alag shreniyon main nivesh ke bajaay keval do vyapak shreniyon main nivesh kii suvidha hogi
 One category will be investment in government securities, which has been raised by $ 5 billion to $ 25 billion and the second category will be corporate bonds
 isamen bhi itani hi vruddhi kar isaki seemaa 51 arab dollar kar di gai he
 Promising further steps towards economic reforms in the coming days, Chidambaram said that the government was steadily and steadily moving towards the next generation of reforms
 chidambaram ne sudhaar prakriya ko badhaane kii disha main uthaaye gaye kadamon kaa zikr karte hue kaha ki haal hi main multibrands khudara kshetra main pratyaksh videshi nivesh kii anumati di gai
 Foreign investment was also liberalized in the aviation and broadcasting sector
 dijal ke daam ko aanshik taur par niyantranmukt kiya gaya or sabsidiukt rasoi gas silendar kii aapurti simit kii gai
 On a question about West Bengal Chief Minister Mamata Banerjee's allegations of discrimination in allocation of central assistance to the states, the Finance Minister said that such allegations are not true
 rajyon ko jo bhi dhan diya jaataa he vah samvidhan main kii gai vyavastha or vittiya ayog kii siforeeshon ke anuroop diya jaataa he
 Chidambaram said, no state is given any priority nor discrimination is done against anyone
 bhedbhaav barte jane ke aarope galat hai or main in aaropon ko khaarij karata hum
 On the question of granting special state status to Bihar, Orissa and some other states, Chidambaram said, "he has never supported the idea of giving special status to states
" haalanki, sarkaar ne rigerv bank ke purv governor vivi reddy kii adhyakshata main gathit 14wein vitt ayog se kaha he ki vah karj ke boj tale dabe rajyon kii samasya par dhyaan dete hue sarkaar ko aavashyak suzav de
 The Finance Minister has told the states that along with creating a better environment to become stronger, the law and order situation should be improved and economic activities should be encouraged
 chidambaram ne kaha ki bazaar niamak sebi kii nilaamee prakriya ke tahat companiyon ke liye bond ke jariye dhan jutaney kii seemaa tay karne kii maujuuda prakriya kaa sthaan avasanrachana (inphra) bond main apanaai jane vaali prakriya le sakati he
 The comments unhone kaha ki jab kabhi jarurat hogi sarkari bond kii seemaa ko badhaayaa jayega
 "when the investment reaches 80 percent of the investment limit for foreign institutional investors in corporate bonds, then the government will review the foreign investment limit to facilitate the investment plan of big investors," he said
 niveshkon ko ek disha dete hue vitt mantri ne kaha, mujhe prasannataa he ki sarkari bond main nivesh vistaar kii salanaa seemaa sarkaar kii bazaar se sakal udhari ke paanch pratishat ke daayre main hi bani hui he
 However, it excludes return purchases
 vaishvik arthvyavastha ke maamle main chidambaram ne kaha ki euroshetra ke sankat se puri duniya main nivesh gatividhiyaan prabhavit hui hai or bharat bhi isse achoota nahin rahaa
 He reminded that 9 of the economic growth in the year 2010-11
 3 pratishat tak pahunchane ke baad arthvyavastha main susti ai or 2011-12 main yah ghatakar 6
 It has been reduced to 2 percent and now during the current financial year it has been estimated to be in the range of 5 percent, the minimum growth in the last decade

 is plan ke jariye ek-ek kar congress-jedies ke vidhayak apni party se istipha dete ja rahe hai or dhire-dhire bijepi kaa khemaa majboot hota ja rahaa he
 Congress MLA from Vijayanagar in Karnataka Anand Singh on Monday resigned the Assembly Speaker Ramesh Kumar
 isi ke kuch hi der ke baad congress ke duusare vidhayak ramesh jarakiholi ne bhi bagawati rukh akhriyaar karte hue istipha fax se bhej diya

 beg in dinon bijepi or modi kii tarif karne main jute hai
 In this way, the number of Congress mlas is continuously decreasing

e
 Shri Ram College of Commerce in 1926
 SRCC ne chaatro ko undergraduate degree 1933 or post graceuate degree 1948 se deni shuru kii
 The college reached North Campus of Delhi University from Daryaganj in 1957 and is still there

com and MA (economics)
 yogata:grajuation main admician lene ke liye 12veen main mili nabanron ke aadhaar par taiyaar kii gai cat of list ke aadhaar par SRCC main admish hota he

 admician prakriya:grejuate or post graceuate program ke liye admician prakriya may-june ke maheene main shuru hoti he

 uske baad merit ke aadhaar par is college main admician liya ja saktaa he

 pracheen kaal ke kis kaal khand main yah vyavastha bahut behatar kaam kar rahi thi or us kaal main shikaayat karne kii kya vyavastha thi jahaan tab ke logon ne jati vyavastha ke bare main shikaayat darj nahin karai
 The ruling class which introduced it as an oppressive system belongs to which period
 vaise to mere jaise hindi medium vaale bhi cast system par sawaal uthaate hai, magar raav sahab kehete hai ki angrejidan bhartiya hamaare samaaj ke jin reeti rivaajon par sawaal uthaate hai, un buraaiyon kii jaden uttar bharat ke saat sau kaal ke muslim shashan main maujuud thim
 Was there not a caste system in the South? is kaal ke dauraan madhyakaalin panditon ne shastron main kadi sharten laga deen, jinaki aalochana karte hue maujuuda buddhijiviyon ne aitihaasik kaaran nahin dekha
 The Indian caste system emerged in response to some basic needs of the complex life of the people in the course of development of civilization
 dhamrshastron ke anusaar samay ke saath jati vyavastha varna vyavastha main samahit ho gai
 Which Dharmashastra is said, it is not mentioned and it is not mentioned when caste became varna
 vaise itihaaskaar raav bataate hai ki varna vyavastha main puri maanavtaa ko dekhte hue insaan ke kaam ko shreniyon main baanta gaya
 Then they differentiate between varna and caste, saying that the caste system speaks of the community and the varna system belongs to a particular person
 varna moksh kii taraf le jaataa he, jabaki jati kisi sabhy samaaj ke bhautik or maavan sansadhano ke prabandhan ke liye he
 You can be born in a caste and acquire another character
 jati vyavastha pidiyon tak parivaar kii samskruti ko banaae rakhti he
 According to the Dharmashastra, all people are Shudra by birth and they acquire varna through rituals
 aadhunik or pashchim vidwaanon ne varna or jati ko nahin samajha
 One can find work without caste, but changing the profession does not change caste
 kahin aap jati or varna main kanphyus to nahin ho rahe
 According to the Mandal Commission report, there are more than five thousand castes in India, but there are only four varnas
 brahman, kshatriya, vaisya or shudra
 Constituent doctor Bhimrao Ambedkar, educated in the West School of Economics and Columbia University, the two leading universities of the West, wrote in the Annihilation of Caste that it is sad that even today the defenders of caste say that the caste system is the name of division of labor 
 ve kehete hai ki shram kaa vibhaajan har sabhy samaaj kaa lakshan he, isliye jati vyavastha galat nahin he
 The first thing is that the caste system is not just a division of labor
 yah mazdooron kaa bhi aapas main vibhaajan he
 a civilized society must of course have a division of labor, but in any civilized society the division of labor has never taken place in an ever-changing groove
 shram kaa vibhaajan kisi prakritik zarurat par aadhaarit nahin tha
 We choose our career from our personal capacity
 jati vyavastha main is system kaa ulanghan hua he

 doctor ambedkar maksarvaadi nahin the or ye bhaashan 1936 kaa he
